< Text>
I've known about the card room in Paso for years it's been around. However, I figured it's only professional gamblers that went in there. To my surprise you don't have to be a professional gambler to enjoy playing the tables. I watched them playing blackjack and thought hmmm I wanna get in on this action. So I bellied up to the table having no idea how to play except to tap the table if I want another card or wave my hand if I didn't want another one. I follow suit (having no clue why I'm tapping or waving on) thankfully there was only two others at that time and they quickly realized the newbie and I got some schooling from all at the table. Awesome group of people in there. Everyone is very friendly. The kitchen crew, the bar crew and the dealers are all so friendly. My first night at the table I went home with $189 woohoo not bad for a newbie with beginners luck. Second time there the table was busier and the other patrons next to me help guide me on what to do and I walked out with  $95 more than i went in with. The third time I was up $90 but started losing and I lost the $90 I was up plus the $30 I put down to start with.... If I'm gonna play here I might as well work here right ;) come see me at the bar and order some yummy grub! Ok not so much grub but more like 5 star food. If that's to much order a side of fettuccini for $5. Or the BLT that is hands down the best I've ever had! <name>Star Cat</name>< Text>
Good drinks, great service, decent atmosphere given COVID-19.  Reason for 4 stars is that the food we had, the platter with shrimp/beef/pork was heavily salted.  Way way way too much salt on these items.  We ate them but, seriously, cut back on the salt and let your guests add their own.  Corn was delicious, zucchini/mushrooms delicious, lime rice (which tasted like lime rice) was also excellent!  Will go again.  UPDATE:  The last 2x we have been here, the Carne Asada is soooooo salty as to be almost inedible.  Even my nephew who went with us recently said it is much too salty.  The rest of the food was ok. We chose to eat at Tu Madres, and we are glad we did,  my son loved the Carne Asada tacos.  My daughter loved the ‚ÄúDragon Taco‚Äù  plate that her tacos were served on,  in fact so much she ordered seconds, something she never does. < review>
Myself and 3 friends went to Tu Madre last night for an early dinner at 4:30. We ordered the guacamole and chips and the Ahi wontons. The Guacamole tasted nice but there were literally only about 2 tablespoons and a large handful of chips served for $10. We all had margaritas which were $11 on happy hour price and what we all got was a tumbler full of ice. 2 of us wanted to order the chicken enchiladas but we were told they were "all out" of them. At 4:30 ? I would think the enchiladas are probably a mainstay of a Mexican restaurant. I ordered a mexi/cobb salad, 1 person ordered the carnitas and 2 ordered the pulpo. We all left the restaurant feeling hungry. Our bill for 2 rounds of drinks, 2 appetizers and 4 main courses was $150 not including a tip. While the food is fresh, the portion sizes are ridiculously small for the prices they are charging. The atmosphere is nice but this restaurant is not good value for money.</review>

< review>
I came in for a physical exam including eye exam, checking for hernia, blood pressure, etc. When I walked into the facility I was greeted and was assisted by Eddie. He told me to fill out some forms and bring them up to him once I have completed. While I was filling out the form, I was observing the people around me including the staff. My heart goes out to Eddie because he was doing 3 tasks at the same time: handling a patient over the phone and 2 patients in front of the counter. It sounded like the patient on the phone with Eddie was very impatient and screaming at him while he was helping out the other 2 patients. Eddie remained calm, apologetic, and explained to the patient on the phone that he was helping 3 people at the same time. As an educator, I have been in Eddie's situation where I had to deal with juveniles and monster parents. Right after I finished filling out the form, I went up to Eddie and handed in the forms. While I was handing the form to Eddie, I told him that he's such a very patience person and thanked him for not letting the impatience person bother him and his work. Thank you for your patience and keeping a professional look, Eddie!

While I was waiting to get called into the room, there was a lady that came to the waiting area and went from patient to patient and asked about how their day was and asked if they want any snacks, drinks, or any assistance. I have never seen this before in a clinic nor a hospital. This really showed me that Concentra really cares for their patients or visitors. I forgot to ask the lady for her name but what she did that day really made me feel like home. Thank you for doing that.

Jessica and Lliana are the two staffs that called me into room to do my exams. They are the sweetest and nicest human being that you'll find in this facility. I feel like I have known them for ages. They do carried a very good conversation with me as well. They smiled a lot which made me feel homey and welcoming. Lliana is such a sweet girl! I didn't have any pockets or nowhere to put my wallet, sunglasses, and my mobile phone. Lliana offered to hold them for me while I took my eye exam. Thank you very much, Lliana. After the eye exam, Jessica and Lliana took me to a room to check on my blood pressure and my hearing. While they were prepping to give the exam to me, I told them that I have never had this kind of experience where I feel like I am wanted in their facility and treated me like a VIP. Those two young ladies have passions of what they're doing, very easy to communicate with, excellent patience, and friendly. Thank you, Jessica and Lliana!

Will I come to this facility again?? Of course, that's only if I have any type of exam at their facility.</review>
